hereafter folowith boke callyd myrroure oure lady necessary relygyous persones fyrste prologue phere begynneth prologue thys presente boke folowynge called oure ladyes myroure viderunt eam filie syon et beatissimam predicauerunt cantice vi wordes writen holy scrypture thus say englyshe doughtres syon haue sene hyr say oure lady haue shewed hyr mooste blessyd whiche wordes holy goste sayth thre thinges longe praysynge oure mooste blessed lady pfyrste prayse hyr whan sayeth doughters syon pthe seconde doo begynne prayse hyr whan sayeth haue sene hyr pthe thyrde maner hyr praysynge whan sayeth haue shewed hyr mooste blessed therfore sayeth doughtres syon haue sene hyr haue shewed hyr moste blessed pfyrste holy goste tellyth prayse lady callyth doughtres syon though chrysten soulles treuly lyue chrysten fayth may called doughtres syon say holy chyrche yet properly ye ar called doughters syon onely ye ar doughtres holy chyrche chrysten byleue chrysten people y also ye doughtres holy relygion mother noryssheth youre soulles grace monastery y named syon therfore ye doughtres bodely syon ought ye doughtres syon gostly syon y moche say comaundement byholdinge ye ought doughtres comaundement meke redy obedyence byddynges god youre reule youre soueraynes ye ought also doughtres byholdynge cotemplacyon specyally byholdynge youre owne wretchednes youre vnkyndenes agenste god charite goodnes dothe ye oughte beholde also shortnes vnstablenes thys lyfe hastynes dethe ferefulnes dome bytternes paynes swyete ioyfull rewardes blysse ye thus good doughtres syon meke obedyence trew beholdynge thynges ar ye well dysposed worthyly prayse oure moste gloryous lady pthe seconde thynge holy goste tellyth wordes y ye ought doo ye begynne prayse oure lady y ye oughte se ye wote well man ne may well shewe worthynes propertyes thynge praysynge therof yf haue fyrste som syght knowlege thinge one meane shall ye condewly shewe outwarde praysyng excellent hyghnes worthynes moste blyssed heuenly quene oure reuerente lady yt full fayre expressed al youre holy seruyce yf ye haue fyrste syght therof inwarde vnderstandinge pbut asmoche many thoughe ye synge rede yet ye se meanynge therof y therefore onely worshyp praysyng oure lorde iesu chryste hys moste mercyfull mother oure lady gostly coforte profyte youre soules haue drawen youre legende youre seruyce enlyshe ye shulde se vnderstodyng therof worthy holy praysynge oure gloryous lady contente therin deuoutely knowyngly synge yt rede yt say yt worshyp pand many place nakyd letter thoughe yt set enlyshe y easy symple soulles vnderstonde expounde yt declare yt openly letter else fourthe wyth gyther pand farthermore ye shulde haue sprytuall loue inwarde delyte deuocyon thys holy seruyce tell cause meanynges eche parte therof say whan come fyrste inuitory tell inuitatory y say yt y namyd set suche place psalmes hympnes antempnes respoces versicle suche declare ar callyd y say hympne y callyd hympne antepmne callyd antempne fourth ar set sayde suche wyse ye may se playnely story sonday eche thynge hys place pof psalmes haue drawen fewe ye may haue rycharde hampoules drawynge englysshe bible ye haue lysence therto palso drawe thynge one englysshe write agayne often fynde eche place onely fyrste place gloria patri declaryd begynnyng matyns sonday maria er gloria tibi domine ende fyrste hympne daye speke nomore therof seruice ofte yt sayde doo suche moste parte pye shall also vnderstonde thys boke y deuyded thre partyes fyrste haue compyled lytell treaty xxiiii chapytres wherein y shewed condycion diuine seruyce whan wyse yt ought sayde songe specyally youre holy seruice heuenly gracyously ordeyned made treatyce y fyrste parte boke seconde parte y youre seuen storyes accordynge seuen dayes wyeke thyrde parte youre mass pand asmoche ye may se boke myrroure praysynges worthines oure moste excellente lady therfore name oure ladyes myroure oure lady shulde se herselfe therin ye shulde se therin myroure styred deuoutly prayse knowe ye fayle praysinges amende tyll ye may come ye may se face face wythouten eny myrroure pand therfore moste dere deuoute systres ye ar spouse oure lorde iesu chryste specyall chosen maydens doughtres moste reuerede mother lyfte vp eyen soulles towarde youre souerayne lady often bysely loke study myrroure lyghtely contynually hastynge rede moche one labouryng knowe rede ye may se vnderstonde holy seruice ye may serue therwyth plesauce lyke goyth dayly thorughe mouthes let yt synke sauoure contynually youre harte pand aboutes may youre harte better occupyed may ye haue holy heuenly medytacyons may haue deper swetter contemplacion beholde story sonday glory blessyd endeles trinite onehed substaunce godhe se hym ioyed euer wythout gloryous lady vnmade loued themselfe pon twesday ye may se adam worthyly made fel wretchydly synne sorow therfore patriarkes prophetes forknowynge oure lady thereby comforted theyre trybulacyons pon wednesday ye may se thys gloriuos lady moche loued longe desyred began come fourthe thys worlde meruelous clene concepcion holy byrthe charyte god heuen mannes helthe charyte lady erthe byrthe pon thurseday ye may ioyfully se excellente vertues holy conuersacyon full fayrenes soulle body maruaylous carnacyon oure lorde iesu chryste pon fryday ye maye se greate vnspe able sorowes sonnes incarnacyon hys byrthe specyally tyme hys moste bytter passyon pon saterday ye may se holy lyfe oure lady namely tyme sonnes passyon vnto assumpcyon taken vp heuen bothe soulle body sette moste nyghe blessed trinyte aboue creature ioye blessed trinyte glorious lady endelesly made ye rede sonday fulfylled effectually dede assumpcyon ye rede saterday pand thus sonday tyll saterday dayly wekely yerely ye ar occupyed wt youre tongue oure ladyes seruyce wherfore ye ought take hede youre myndes besy cotynually occupyed aboute thinges inwarde vnderstondynge deuocyon cause loke often ryght often thys oure ladyes myrroure yt maye sothefastely veryfyed doughtres syon hathe sene pthe thyrde thynge holy gooste shewyth sayde wordes maner ye shall prayse oure mooste reuerende gloryous lady y openly mekely deuoutly openly ye owghte prayse dystynctely folke may vnderstonde youre praysyng theyr edyfycacyon therfore sayeth haue shewyd thyng shewyd made open folkes knowlege ye ought also pray se mekely yt open shewynge praysynge ye seke worshyp youre owne therfore saythe haue shewyd hymselfe deuoutly also ye ought prayse beholdinge youre mynde tyme youre praysynge inwarde loue deuocyon glorious excellente blyssyd y aboue creature whome ye prayse therefore saythe haue shewyd mo e blessyd pand ye ought euer thanke prayse worshyp god hathe made reuerende lady gracious glorious good hath gyuen moche worshyp excellence power aboue hys creature hath callyd specyally seruyce hath gyue open knowlege moste hyghe excellent worthynes greate benyfytes ye oughte euer cotyneually ioye god prayse heuely kynge namely wt hys holy dyuyne seruyce prophete psalter exhorteth saythepsal cx ix filie syon exultent rege suo laudent nomen eius choro saye doughters syon muste ioye theyre king must prayse name ye quier pand ye ar thus occupied godly praysinges tymes also namely whe ye ar moste nygh kynge youre quiene praye hert lowly ar shall com loke myrroure lyke trew charyte soulles helth cofort forsothe hathe styred thys laboure none erthly thynge ye vouchesafe youre tender charyte hartely praye oure right poure full wretched soulle oure mercyful lorde iesu chryste clenseyt cure yt wt medycyne hys mercy grau te yt euer ioye delyte loue hym hys mooste worthy mother nothynge else lorde meane gloryous vyrgynhys mother maye graunte lyueth rayneth wyth father wyth holygooste endeles god amen phere endyth fyrste prologue begynneth seconde yt lyght euery man drawe eny longe thyng latyn oure englyshe tongue y many wordes latyn haue propre englyssh accordynge therto suche wordes muste turnyd sentence may beste vnderstondyd therfore though laboure kepe bothe wordes sentence boke farre oure language wyll well assente yet tyme folowe sentence wordes mater asketh also many wordes haue dyuerse vnderstodynges tyme ar taken one wyse time som tyme may taken dyuerse wyse one reson clause dyuerse wordes also dyuerse scryptures ar set vnderstode tyme wyse auctoures gramer tell speke oure language also dyuerse yt selfe comen maner spekyng englysshe cotre skante vnderstondid cotre lode pand cause suche yf persones holde selfe conyng whan onely lytell gramer lytel latyn scarcely wel ar bolde catche mannes saynge hys wrytynge wolde many wyse clerkes therfore yf eny suche parsone happen se boke eny oure drawyng fynde eny thynge therin drawen hys entente therfore redy blame yt say yt wroge cousell symplenes seke soulles fode take lytell hede hys saynges wyttynge well wyser eny man y better wyll aduysed blame mannes studdy lesse good presuptuous wyll fynde defaulte depraue ye often tymes tho thynges vndersto dyth therfore holde selfe wyse may contente wyth theyr owne wysdome began thys werke nothynge edyfycacyo yt fele symplely owne wyttes loue enformyd wyser seint hierome ye wynde though hys harte stretched wt brenyng charite god blather full wynde swete harte brenyng gat knowlege wordes saynges whiche coulde shulde make resposes antemps hympnes ordeyne soge note ether therfore though youre legende longe lesso red one alone yet thinke voyde tyme wyll ye ought tyme sytfull stylle eche worde red wt full greate dylygence deuoute entendauce therto sekeyng haue deuocio body oure lorde pthat ye ought nether slowe chyrche warde ne hasty go thense capi xi therfore haue helthe strengthe ar lettyd obedience ought full hasty redy come holy seruyce lothe thense oughte spare eny slowth dulnes body ne yet though fele tyme maner payne stomacke hed lacke sleape indygestyon quycly aryse loue goddes seruice feruently dyspose therto shulde fynde lordes helpe often fynde selfe better ease sone bothe body soule yf lay fauoure flesshe styl withdraw thense pforlyke styrre vp themselfe wyth quycke feruent wyll thyde warde ar holpe fourth comforted oure lordes good aungels man sodenly afrayde turned agayne ran chyrche fast myght lyke man hal e mad hys wytte dreade come hys stalle stode whyle trembelyng pantyng sone fel downe grounde lay styll dede longe tyme felyng dyuine seruyce wolde synge wt monkes also wolde cope stande synge chantoure myddes ye quier wherof hapned tyme whan beseged castel rebel agenst hym feaste saynt anyan fell tyme orleauce lefte hoste sege went thyder toke cope songe myddes ye quier wote came agn dei begone yt thryes wt hygh voyce knelyng doune yche tyme hys knee walles ye castell beseged fell downe sodenly groude castel dystroyed youre houres longe many thynges fyrste yt sayd wt clene coseyence yf erthely lorde loue haue tho seruautes yt ar nexte honest clene theyr gouernance aray moche yt longeth lorde lordes haue hys seruauntes clene wtout fylthe synne namely ar called cotynually occupyed holy praysyng therfore sayth prophete dauid deo nostro sit locuda decora que laudacio psal cxlvi god may geuen ioyfull fayre praysynge fayre ioyfull wel set gyther may soulle verely ioye ye praysyng god yf yt fyrste made fayre clensed synne pwherfore hathe remorse coscyence dedly synne therwt saith syngeth goddes seruice synneth sayngde celeb mi capitulo grau clement yet yf lefte yt vnsayde shulde synne greuosly shall syth synneth bothe doyng leueynge thus shall ought repente syn ful wyl purpose shryue hym therof amende lowly meke hym god aske hym forgyuenes trustyng lordes mercy shall say hys seruyce wt sorow harte mekenes drede ought thynke yt y dedly synne cotrite sory theroflibro secundo capitulo xi pand hereof ye haue notable example saynt maudes reuelacios bothe diuine seruyce howslyng lyke man agenst lordes comyng hym maketh clene house yf may hast cast ye vnclenesse entrey swepeth yt vp togyther corner castyth yt oute afterwarde ryghte whan persone goyth dyuyne seruyce howslynge felyth grudgeyng coscyence yf may get gostly father shryue hym ought sorowe hys synnes harte contricion shryue therof god swepe yt corner hys mynde tyll may gette hys confessour trustynge oure lordes mercy go hys seruice hys howslyng pthis kepte time synnes dyuyne seruyce also kepte youre howslynge suche dayly defaultes neglyge ce ye ar syker ar dedly pbut eny know himselfe gylty dedly synne owght howsled tyl shryuen also dyuyne seruice yf eny fele remorse dedly synne wyttyng well yt dedly synne yf may esely get hys confessoure begyn hys seruice ought shryuen take hys penaunce trew shryfte mouthe wt absolucion folowyng lyghtyth moche soulle gyueth conforte hope forgyuenes wherby may frely deuoutly wythout entendaunce hartesuper psalmo qui ha itat sermone xvi isidore saythlibro tercio e sumo beno ca xii prayer longeth harte lyppes god takyth hede ye harte wordes ptherfore say theyr seruyce occupy theyre minde ther whyle thinges ar lyke man payeth hys dette wyth false money semeth golde syluer wythout y coper bra wythin whiche contentyth lorde payeth yt rather uoketh hym dysplesaunce wylfully purpose occupyeth mynde tyme holy houres thynges takyth hede sayth syngeth yf gyue stede wylfully without nede herynge seynge otherwyse eny thynge wherby distracte fro mynde aduertence ye seruyce saith though say syngfully wordes ro cap gr ni clement yet payeth treuly hys dette ne pleasyth god therwyth offendyth hym synneth greuously ought penaunce therfore say seruyce agen better entendaunce doyng penaunce bothe place vnderstandyth repentaunce harte shryfte wyth fulfyllynge suche penaunce hys goostly father enioyneth hym yt standyth hys dyscrescyo enioyne hym penaunce hys neglygence therwyth enioyne hym say seruyce agen thynge stede therof bothe case lyke folowe hym semeth moste spedefull hys soulles heltheinno de celeb misse ca pmo nethelesse yf haue sayde seruyce agen come shryfte shal enioyned say yt agen shall haue penauce fyrste myssayngro capitulo graui cleme pbut dressyth hys harte god begynnyng hys seruyce wt wyll purpose kepe mynde stable thervpo though yt happen hym afterwarde neglygence fraylte dystracte hys thoughtes sayeth besyde hys fyrste purpose yf abyde wylfully suche thoughtes hath perceyued turnyth hys mynde ageyne hys seruyce y sory therof whiche roted loge yuel custome frayle wretched soulle boude borne doune yt yt sturre vp yt selfe fro wandryng vagant thoughtes yt accustomyd man rennyth downewarde fro hye hyl may stynte hymselfe one goynge tyll comethe vale ryght haue vsed theyre harte renne downewarde yt wyll vpon erthly vayne thynges lyghtly stynte yt ne gather yt stablenessup ioh trac xlix yuel custome saynt austyn sayth therfro therfore remedy agenste muste sharpenes drede quycknes hope soulle dysposed pfor lyght harted vayne condicyons nedeth case vse mynde bysely thoughtes drede hys deth hys dome paynes beholdynge praysynge god yt brennyth hym woudeth hym sore though suffer soulle haue soe peace eny tymes non seyth yt turne prayer go goddes seruice rennyth laboureth hys myghtes brynge worldely vayne yuel thoughtes besynes mynde scater harte deuocyo make hym lese ye fruyte hys prayersermone quarto de ieinnio saynte bernarde sayth effectuall spedeful prayer yf yt done yt oughte felly bysely laboureth malycyous enemy lette yt premedy agenste y make vpon brest pryuely contyneually suche tymes token crosse wyth stronge stedfaste faythe paciently perceuerantly laboure kepe holde mynde vpon lorde vpon tyme goddes seruyce lette bothe hymselfe capi xvii thys malycyous serpent seeth thus chased many dryue way seketh entre agayne way assayeth gette holde one whome sturrethe anone make vayne chere synge token wherby one tyme many ar meued maner dyssolucyon dystracte sadnes inwarde deuocyo sturreth make somwey warde token thynge comberously thrughe ar taryed theyre myndes troubeled theyre spyrytes ar dryuen quyetnes deuocyon anguysshe paynefull grudginges haste faster theyre armure begynne gyue batayle suche vayne troubelous sturrynges laboure gather holde theyr mynde gyther sayde else subtyll enemy wyll enter vpon theym ageyne pand therfore suche vayne comberous people ar fourthe cause make dystraccyon goddes seruyce fendes chyldren fulfyl hys desyre may brynge aboute hymselfe oure lorde sayth hys gospel vos ex patre diabolo estis et desideria patris vestri vultis facere ioan viii ye ar chyldren father fende ye wyll desyres youre father pif kynge meate hys seruantes aboute hym serue hym yf feylde fyghte hys knyghtes hym warre hym yf laboures hys vyne yerde hys gardyn came one made hys seruantes knyghtes hys laboures skatered flye seruice shulde suche one called traytor kynge put dothe moche parlously ar traytours god vanyte trouble cause dystraccyon hys holy seruyce make myndes trew knyghtes laboures skatered pthese ar bad felowes let comon profyt theyre felyshyp lyke vnto father veryly forgyue oure trespassoures desyre forgyuen et ne no inducas temptacionem nd lede v temptacyon suffer v oure vnkyndenesse demerytes falle synne eny temp acyon thys y petycyon hartely selfe lese grace deuocio haue gotten foude prayer goddes seruyce may one cause ye ende eche houre seruyce lady ye grete wt salutacio gabriel elysabeth ye dyd ye begynnynge say aue maria heyle mary full grace god y wt blyssed thow amongest woman blyssed fruyte thy wombe oute ende poratio omnipotens almyghty endeles god haste vouched safe borne v ye moste chaste virgyn pray make v serue wt chast body plese wt meke harte pa fayre knyttynge gyther chaste body meke soulle chaste body may serue god yt plese god wtout meke harte ne chast kepte body soulle wythout mekenesse oramus ette pray moste mercyfull vyrgyn mary quene worlde aungels thow gette refresshyng whome fyre purgatory purgyth synne r forgyuenesse rightwyse people perseuerauce good defende v frayle presente pareyles yo say pareylles cotynewally falle vnto v per eundem oure lorde iesu cryste amen pat pryme veneranda hympne ye aske ye blyssed trynyte prayer lady haue lyghte grace wherby ye may se flee yuell doo good pryme faythe gretly ympugned heretykes holy man called atthanasius bysshop alysaundre made thys psalme strengthe ryghte faythe agenst heretykes coforte enformacio thme trew byleue therfore holy chyrche moche blyssed trynyte pantempne speciose po fayrest shape sonnes men woman sonne clene vnspotted vyrgyn make v go contynewally bypathe thy lawe wythout spotte synne pthere y dyfference bytwyxte hyghe waye bypathe hyghe waye y large commune therby vnderstonded comaundementes oure lorde muste kepe wyll saued bypatthe vnderstonde cousayles longe relygyous folke perfeccyon pthe chapyter nec est virgo holy gloryouse vyrgyn god lorde thynges hathe loued responce iesu christe iesu cryst sonne god lyue haue mercy v uerse qui natus borne vyrgyn marye uersycle os pro nobis pray v holy mother god answere vt digni made worthy grace chryste poryson sanctum maria holy mary mother oure lorde iesu cryst benygne god perpetuall vyrgyn quene heuen vouchesafe wyth sayntes chosen god pray v oure lorde god father allmyghty mo e deserue holpen saued heled socoured defended hym lyueth rayneth god parfyt trynyte wythoute ende amen benedicamus domino blysse oure lorde deo gratias thanke god pat tyerse antempne auerte oculos turne awaye oure yne mooste honeste mother se vanyte informe v dyscyplyne lernynge thy sonne hys handes made v pthe chapyter ab initioeccless xxliii chapiter sayde persone oure ladye thus ab initio endelesly tymes made shall neuer fayle holy dwellynge haue mynystred hym thys y thus mene endelesly tymes forknowen ordeyned god made forknowyng god tolde openly legende daye wryten shall neuer fayle neyther soule eny synne ne body eny corrupcio lady holy body turned corrupcion erthe take vp knytte soule glorye heuen holy dwellynge haue mynystred serued hym yt holy dwellynge whan lorde iesu crist dwelled mother wombe mynystred vnto hym mater holy body yt also holy dwellynge lorde iesu crist lady moder ioseph dwelled togyther one howse oure lady serued blyssed sone esu cryst mete drynke clothe ful plesa te seruice blyssed trynyte father sonne holy goste yt also holy dwellynge goddes seruautes dwelle togyther cogregacio charite lorde thu crist myddes amo gest math xviii hymselfe sayth hys gospell lady mynystreth helpe grace ful besyly myghte serue sone plesure therfore sayth holy dwellynge haue mynystred byfore hym respoce inclina bowe th ere v quene heuens uerse ad quam whome lorde lordes bowed hymselfe v uersycle esto nobis v helper forsake v answere nec despicias ne dyspyce v hye lady pof thys psalme de profundis wt oryson folowynge de profundis ye haue monastery beer graue cotynually syghte beer mynde dethe graue mynde laste dome bodyes shall aryse theyre graues token therof abbesse castyth oute lytel erthe tow fyngers soulle body vnderstonded tow fyngers sondered dethe shall knytte ageyne togyther euerlastyngely shall aryse ioye payne pthys arysynge begonne resurreccyon lorde iesu cryst shall ended ye ende worlde thereof y made mencyon bothe thys psalme de profundis oryson domine sancte pater foloweth pand therfore eche day tyerce ye go thys graue brynge dethe youre dome mynde ye begynne speke occupyed aboute eny thynge ye shulde nothynge say ne day ye dare dye anon therwyth appere oure lordes dome ye pray father heuen kepte holy body hys sonne iesu cryste clene graue rered yt vp thyrde day vouchesafe kepe youre bodyes clene hys seruyce gouerne eche day whyle ye lyue worlde laste dome bodyes may aryse amongest reproued amongest hys chosen soulles wyth bodyes ioye wt hym euerlastyngly pand ende thys prayer ye saye nomine patris et fil et spiritus sancti y name father sonne holy goste thys y sayd onely ende prayer begynnyng dedes wordes workes day folowynge shulde haue theyr begynnynge sayde done name worshyp blyssed trynyte pfor thoughe cotyneuall scylence maner ended oure ladyes masse y done yet place ye ar y quyer causyth yt cotynued til tyme ye shulde begyn goddes name warely kepe day vnder hys drede ye alwaye redy go youre graue pand ye haue prayed hym feruente desyre bothe mattyns masse youre seruyce asked hym suche grace mercy ye thynke nede youre selfe therfore ye aske tho prayer herde spedde letted synnes eny others whe ye saypsal cxxix de profundis lorde haue cryed vnto depnesse lorde voyce pall thys worlde y depe pryso heuen synne yuel depnesse namely loue abyde therin cry helpe beholdynge theyr owne synnes throwe downe themselfe depnesse mekenesse repentaunce sorowful desyre aske mercy crye well lorde fro depnesses pthys psalme y syxte seuen psalmes eleuenthe fyftene psalmes six nombre perfeccyon god made thynges syx dayes eleuen y nombre trespace yt goeth ten y nombre goddes lawe hys comaudementes therfore syx eleuen come togyther vpon thys psalme y none parfyt erthe hathe hym trespace synne nedeth cry god mercy helpe fiant aures tue thyne eres mote take hede vnto voyce prayer ye say lorde voyce thyne eres mote voyce prayer yt al one sentence yt y sayde twyes shew gretenesse nede freuoure desyre nothyng lettyth grace spede prayer synne therfore ye allegge hym thre caw sturre hym notwythstandynge eny synne fyrste cause y comon fraylte feblenesse man may dereche rygoure doume synne deserueth thefore ye say si iniquitates thow wayte streyghtly oure synnes wyckednesses punysshe rigoure dome lorde shall bere yt suffre yt shulde say y none lyue may escape payne gette blysse therfore thy rigoure may answere deserue yt must tempered thy mercy quia apud te ag ste y mercy sacrifyce apese thys seconde thynge ye allegge herde spedde youre prayer youre merytes mercy mean passyon oure lorde iesu cryste sacryfysed hys moste holy precyous bloude y contynewally syghte father heuen apease hym agenste mankynde therfore ye say agenste y mercy sacryfyce apese pthen ye allegge thyrde cause saye et propter legem tuam thy lawe lorde haue suffred abyden yf ye sayde haue kepte thy lawe therfore abyde thy rewarde yf kepe byddeth may sewer haue promyseth byddeth forgyue myseth youre synnne shall forgyuen yf forgyue may sewerly aske forgyuenesse mercy oure synnes yf gyue helpe well hym may sewerly aske helpe grace endeles blysse hym sayeth gyue shall gyuen vnto forbere suffer wyl spare v oure deseruynge hys beheste therfore ye saye sustinuit sowlle hathe su red hys worde sowlle hathe hoped lorde lyke sowlle suffereth pacyently wronges contraryous thinges obedyence worde hope rewarded trouthe hys worde howe longe shulde ye thus suffer abyde hope custodia matutina kepynge morowe tyde vnto nyghte israel mote hope lorde pthe morowe tyde kepeynge y oure yonge age come yeres dyscrecio knowe good yuel kepe v yuel good tylle tyme chyldes lyfe y yt nyghte vnknowynge begynneth morowe tyde kepeynge nyghte folowynge y oure dethe tyme morowe tyde yonge age vnto nyghte dethe israel y say eche good crysten man oughte wylfully suffer penauce laboure trybulacio hope rewarded labourer trauayleth day hope haue hys hyre euen day hys lyfe ordeyned labour suffer seke haue rewarde endelesse reste ioye lyfe foloweynge palso thys morowe tyde kepynge y vnderstonde resurreccyon oure lorde iesu cryste arose morowe tyde knyghtes kepte hys sepulcre nyghte y vnderstonded day doume shall aryse hys chosen shall taken endelesse blysse body sowle lyke y gloryfyed heuen sowlle body hys resurreccyo paste oures come veryly y arysen veryly shall aryse therfore glad shulde euery crysten soulle suffer laboure hys body penauce trybulacyon hope brynge yt glory resurreccyon haue synned suffycient make full amendes ne deserue haue ioye yet yf haue good wylle suffer may oughte sewrely hope quia apud dnm ageynste lorde y mercy plentyous redempcyon lacketh v raunsome y suffycyente paye v onely dresse v parteners therof et ipse shall agenby israel fro hys wyckednesses hys synnes therfore ye thanke blyssed trynyte wyth gloria patri pthe oryson domine sacte pater lorde holy father keptest body whyche thow toke thy sone vyrgyn mary vnhurte graue arreredyst yt vp vncorrupte beseche kepe bodyes ene vndefowled thy holy seruice dresse way thys tyme greate ferefulle daye doume cometh may ed amongest thy sayntes soulles mote ioye endelesly deserue felowed thy chosen name father sone holy goste amen pat sexte antempne omnia mandata hyest god thy comaundementes ar trouthe therfore thy gyfte thy worde mote launterne oure fete gloryous prayer thy moste worthy mother pthe chapyter egredietur rodde shall sprynge rowte iesseesaie xi oute rowte therof shall sprynge vp flowre thervpon shall reste spyryte lorde spyryte wysdome vnderstondynge spyryte cousayle strengthe spyryte knowynge pytye spyryte drede lorde shall fulfyl hym piesse father kynge dauyd whose lynage came oure lady therfore called rodde came oute rowte iesse oute spronge flowre oure lorde iesu cryste vpo whome rested moste excellence seuen gyftes holy goste ar named nombred pa nother chapyter ecclesi xxiiii et sic insyon sewrely se e stabled syon haue rested also halowed cytye ierusalem y power pthese wordes ar redde bothe oure lorde iesu cryste also oure lady haue hym y named three place syon cytye ierusalem syon y moc e say beholdynge y vnderstonde sowles gyuen contemplacyon oure lorde iesu chryste y sewrely stabled trowbled aboute many thynges pby halowed cytye y vnderstonded sowlles gyuen actyfe lyfe wherin oure lorde iesu restyth charyte haue theyre euen crysten cyte y moche say one hed cytezyns yt sayde halowed purenesse entente offer god theyr workes pby ierusalem vnderstonde prelate gouernoures haue power cure vpon bothe cotemplatyf actyfe lyfe therfore theyr lyfe called meddelyd lyfe meane betwene actyfe cotemplatyf hauynge parte withe bothe oughte se bothe kepte peace accordynge theyr callynge therfore ar vnderstonde ierusalem moche say ye syghte peace oughte haue sighte wysdome dyscrecio canne kepe peace partyes ende hathe parted wt owne power therfore saythe ierusalem y power responce eternum worde hyest father abydeth without ende uerse quod whiche hathe dwelled halle maydens wombe phere vnderstondeth worde endelesse worde father oure lorde iesu cryste uersycle da nobis lady gyue v chastyte body sowlle ne vn que neuer offende sone thy chastyte pat none antempne reconcilia reconcyle v vyrgyn mother thy rightewys sone erre shepe hathe peryshed hys mercyes many pthe chapyter borateesai xlv dew heuens aboue cloudes e rayne ryghtwys erth mote opened bery sauyour rightwysnes myghte aryse gether hym lorde made hym pby heuens ar vnderstode aungels dewed aboue gabryel cam downe wyth salutacyon oure lady clowdes ar vnderstode prophetes rayned wt besy prophesy comynge lorde iesu cryste erthe y vnderstonde lady opened co sente gabryels gretynge bare sauyoure iesu cryst whome spronge ryghtwysnes say grace maketh man ryghteful lorde vnderstode father heuen made oure lorde iesu hys manhode rede nowe ageyne chapiter ye shall fynde yt playne easy vnderstonde pa nother chapyter ecclesi xxiiii et radicaui haue fastned route people worshyped herytage people cotrees god abydyng fulnes sayntes p crysten people y worshyped aboue people konwlege ryghte byleue sacrametes holy chyrche therfore lady roted spual helpe fauoure namely suche seke theyr chefe herytage heuen erthe also lady abydeth fulnesse saintes neuer saynte erthe ne augel heuen y full vertues grace lady hathe fulnesse perfeccyo therfore sayth saynt bernarde uerely sayth abydynge fulnesse sayntes fayled faythe patriarkes ne spyryte prophetes ne zele apostels ne ye stablenesse martyr ne sobernesse confessoures ne chastyte vyrgyns ne ye plenteousnesse wedded ne clenesse aungels responce pax multa moche pea loueth law maydens fone uerse et non hurte occasyon euerlastynge worshyp uersycle errauimus haue erred shepe peryshed reduxit good shepeherde vyrgyn bare hathe broughte v ageyne pof euensonge indulgete ar certayne houres dyuyne seruyce longeth day pryme tyerce sexte none certayne lo ge nighte euensoge coplyn mattyns euensonge fyrst howre longeth nighte therfore yt called songe euen begynnynge nighte yt hathe hys name latin euen sterre apperyth euen pnow yt man y frayle vnstable hymselfe thynge plesyth one tyme yt dysplesyth hym nother tyme wyll wyll yt sone reaso desyreth sensualyte agayne fayth soule wolde haue flesshe contraryeth sythe one man y thus contraryous dyuerse hymselfe meruayle thoughe many men gatheryd togyther often tymes dyuerse cotrary felynges co dycios wherof riseth amongest somtyme trouble grudgeynges harte worde chere dede pbut though yt oure power ape alwayes sotyme take occasio wherby ar ed ageynste sotyme thynges take occasyon meued ageynste v yet yt power grace cosente wylfully suche sturrynges ire vnpacyence namely besy hasty put remedy ageynst redy forgyue eny thinge y done ageynste v sone aske forgyuenes fele eny y hurte v therfore saynte austyne byddeth hys rewlecapitulo vi shulde haue stryues else shulde sone ende meane thoughe moued fraylete harte eny vnpacyence shulde notte geue suche stede therto breke oute wt wordes stryfe yf ouersene breke oute stryffe muste haste v make ende thereof redy forgyfyng askynge forgyfnesse lenger suche forgyfynge askynge forgyfnesse taryed lenger endureth harte sturryng ire lenger endure encrese tyl sowleys ouercome grace withdrawyth fende enteryth therfore sayeth saynte pauleephesi iiii sol non occidat super iracundiam vestram et nolite locum dare diabolo y saye suffer wrathe abyde tylle sonne goynge downe wylleth geue place fende kepyth wrathe harte y occupyed wyth yuell bytter thoughtes whereby fende catchyth holde brynge hym worsecapitulo xiii ptherfore saynte benet ordeyned hys rewle eche day ende mattyns begynnynge daye laste ende euensonge begynnynge nyghte pryoure name shulde saye lowde pater noster myghte yt saynge petycyon sayeth et dimitte nobis y gyue v oure trespaces forgyue trespace v shulde sturred drawen forgyue eche othercapitulo iiii pfor cause hathe lorde ordeyned holy rewle ye shulde euery day bynnyng euensoge eche forgyue aske forgyuenes saynge lowde harte tongue indulgete nobis forgyue v god hys moste mercyfull mother mary yf haue offended wt worde dede sygne token yf eny trespace agenste v wyth moste full wylle harte forgyue yt pand thys ye say aue maria oure lady therby ye shulde stroge breke downe cotrarious sturrynges ye may forgyue veryly harte lyke ye say mouthe pand thys ye saye euensonge rather eny youre howres cause euensonge begynnynge nyghte said therfore sonne shulde go downe vpon youre wrathe pareyles haue rehersed ye forgyue aske forgyuenes tyme occasyons trespaces hathe hapned day ye may clene pesyble coscience praygod wt youre euensonge holy seruyce oughte sayde wyth clene restefull harte pif eny ouercome wyth temptacyon ire whyche god forfende wolde say thys indulgete cause wolde forgyue gretly blame yet neuer ye excused yt sayd name therfore byndethe whether saye yt saye yt whether thense therfore absente saye theyre euensonge alone oughte neuer lesse say yt thoughe none presente speke yet speke name al vnyte congregacyon forgyuenesse asked offered ye may wytte eche person sayeth forgyue eche one spake onely owne name shulde saye forgyue forgyue also yf yt sayd vnyte stande tone syde shulde forgyue eche speke gyther ouer tother syde themselfe yt shulde seme eche one sayeth yt name vnyte therfore yt byndeth forgyue pardoneth theyr trespace therfore wretched persone eny way wardenes harte wolde vnreconcyled dysceuered holy vnyte tyme pthys y dayely sacryfyce ye offer euery daye god euensonge tyme fygured contyne wall sacrifyce god bad moyses shulde offered dayly hym euen songe tymeexodi xxix sone goynge downe sayd wolde dwelle amongest theyr lorde god shulde well know theyr lorde god ptherfore sewre may ye ye shall haue oure lorde god ye wylle aske hym youre helthe yf ye gette hym dwelle thus amongest dayly offerynge thys sacryfyce charyte vnyte pbut nowe perauenture ye myghte aske whether thys askynge forgyuenesse thys indulgete suffycient eny trespace offence eny dothe agenste nother without eny specyal askeynge pto thys answere persone agenste whome trespace offence done oughte indulgete saide quier whether bere wylfully eny heuines harte make shew eny heuynes worde dede agenste persone yt hathe offended far offece logeth owne selfe owne cause though ye aske neuer forgyuenesse ne trespaces yt ar done agenste god agenst relygyo oughte correcte rewles relygyon tyme y netheles indulgete ware none kepe wrathe ne make quarell owne cause vnder coloure relygyon zele obseruaunces therof personal cause far hurte relygyon ar forgyuen indulgete y sayde thys ye may se wordes ye say eny trespace ageynste v wyth moste full wyll forgyue yt therfore eny forgyue wyll harte wordes ar sayd makyth gabbynge thoughe say wordes herselfe ne sayd ar sayde quyer name bynde sayde pbut parsone hathe wyttyngly offended nother oughte y reconcyled aske forgyuenesse knoweth hathe offended indulgete begynne yf wyl thoughe forgyue yt indulgete oughte speke therof yet muste aske forgyuenesse afterwarde ye souerayne serches haue cure relygyon oughte se sadly correcte onely trespace yt dyd agenste syster moche obstynasy obedyence agenste intente rewle wolde seke recocyled breketh vnyte congregacyon myghte cause oure lorde wythdrawe hys gracious presence loueth dwelle vnyte restful soulles also geueth way enmy take power ouer selfe dysceuereth herselfe vnyte holy congregacyon shepe wandereth alone vnyte flocke y sone taken deuoured wolfe ye y sayde wyll forgyue namely tyme indulgete pand therfore eche one oughte full ware yt kepe ne bere grudgeynge ne wrate harte though eny man hyde yt tyme warde shewynge god knoweth yt well ynoughe wythdrawyth hys grace fende catchyth holde sowle pnow happes somme myghte thynke shall wolde fayne forgyue loke yt ye saye wythout feynynge ye wolde forgyue veryly harte ye forgyue thoughe ye fele neuer many contrary sturynges ye folowe ye sturynges worde ne dede veryly dyspleased lothe compelle youre selfe contrary suche frowarde sturynges hurte ye sowle haue oure wylle free oure felynges therfore may wylle wylle v lyste maye fele ne vnfele v lyste therfore oure mercyfull lorde takyth v oure felynges oure wylles pnetheles though persone felte many bytter sturrynges ire vnpacyence yf dysplesauce ther arose ageynste wyth myghty feruente wylle prayed oure lorde hys holy mother helpe wente chyrche sayde aue maria indulgete wyth couente hope gette grace ouercome hymselfe trowe prayer oure lady obedyence rewle knyttynge hymselfe vnyte congregacyo shulde fele fersenesse hys sturrynges sone abated pthus therfore recocyled gither ye begynne youre euensonge ye say fyue psalmes haue forgyuenesse ye haue offended god youre fyue wyttes meryte lordes fyue woundes
